## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Map Test Coverage Gaps in Kafka Consumer Group Coordinator

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/kafka--e678b4b (mirror of apache/kafka)
**Output:** Write your analysis to `/workspace/coverage_analysis.md`

## Objective

Identify test coverage gaps in Kafka's consumer group coordinator. The group coordinator manages consumer group membership, partition assignment, and offset commits for Kafka consumers.

## Scope

Focus on:
- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.scala` — main coordinator logic
- `core/src/test/scala/unit/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorTest.scala` — existing tests
- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadata.scala` — group state machine

## Content Expectations

Your analysis must:
1. **Identify at least 5 specific failure modes** that are not tested in `GroupCoordinatorTest.scala`
2. **Propose a regression test** for each failure mode (class name, test method signature, key assertions)
3. **Estimate the coverage delta** each proposed test would add (which code paths would it hit)
4. **Label risk level**: HIGH / MEDIUM / LOW

## Output Format

Write to `/workspace/coverage_analysis.md`:

```markdown
# Test Coverage Gap Analysis: Kafka Consumer Group Coordinator

## Summary

## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests

### Failure Mode 1: [Name]
- **Risk**: HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW
- **Code Location**: GroupCoordinator.scala ~line NNN
- **Description**: [What failure scenario is untested]
- **Proposed Test**:
  ```java
  @Test
  public void testXxx() { ... }
  ```
- **Coverage Delta**: [Which code paths this test would exercise]

[Repeat for 5+ failure modes]

## File References
```

- Each gap must reference a specific file and approximate location
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

| 7 | `onMetadataUpdate` null-argument guards (`Objects.requireNonNull`) are never triggered by tests | **LOW** | lines ~2241–2242 |

Let me analyze what's tested and what's not.\n\n**What's already tested in GroupCoordinatorServiceTest.java:**\n\n1. `testStartupShutdown` - startup/shutdown lifecycle\n2. `testConsumerGroupHeartbeat*` - consumer group heartbeat (valid, not started, with exceptions, request validation)\n3. `testStreamsGroupHeartbeat*` - streams group heartbeat (valid, not started, with exceptions, validation, unsupported features)\n4. `testShareGroupHeartbeat*` - share group heartbeat (valid, not started, with exceptions, validation)\n5. `testPartitionFor` - partition assignment\n6. `testGroupMetadataTopicConfigs` - topic configs\n7. `testOnElection` - partition election \n8. `testOnResignation*` - partition resignation\n9. `testJoinGroup*` - join group (valid, with exception, invalid group ID, not started, invalid session timeout)\n10. `testSyncGroup*` - sync group (valid, with exception, invalid group ID, not started)\n11. `testHeartbeat*` - classic heartbeat (valid, coordinator not available exception, coordinator exception, not started)\n12. `testLeaveGroup*` - leave group (valid, UnknownMemberIdException, not started)\n13. `testListGroups*` - list groups (valid, with failure, not coordinator, when not started, empty partitions)\n14. `testConsumerGroupDescribe*` - consumer group describe (valid, invalid group ID, coordinator load in progress, coordinator not active)\n15. `testStreamsGroupDescribe*` - streams group describe (valid, invalid group ID, coordinator load in progress, coordinator not active)\n16. `testDescribeGroups*` - describe groups (valid, invalid group ID, coordinator load in progress, not started)\n17. `testFetchOffsets*` - fetch offsets (valid with different combinations, not started, with wrapped errors)\n18. `testDeleteOffsets*` - delete offsets (valid, invalid group ID, with exception, not started)\n19. `testDeleteGroups*` - delete groups (valid, with exception, not started, plus share group variations)\n20. `testCommitTransactionalOffsets*` - transactional offset commits (not started, invalid group ID, valid, with wrapped error)\n21. `testCompleteTransaction*` - complete transaction (valid, not started, unexpected partition)\n22. `testOnMetadataUpdate*` - metadata update (not started, schedules operations when topics deleted, no operations when no deletions, swallows errors)\n23. Heartbeat request validation tests\n\n**What's NOT tested:**\n\n1. **`commitOffsets` error cases when coordinator is NOT started** - The test only covers the basic happy path and `nullGroupId` check. There's no test for when `commitOffsets` is called and the runtime throws `NotLeaderOrFollowerException` or `KafkaStorageException` (which should return `NOT_COORDINATOR`).\n\n2. **`commitOffsets` - null vs empty group ID behavior** - The code handles `null` groupId but allows empty string (\"\") to pass through. The `isGroupIdNotEmpty` check is used for most operations, but `commitOffsets` only checks for null (not empty string). There's no test for committing offsets with an empty string group ID.\n\n3. **`describeShareGroupOffsets`/`describeShareGroupAllOffsets` - when `metadataImage == null`** - Both methods return `COORDINATOR_NOT_AVAILABLE` when `metadataImage` is null. There's no test for this specific code path.\n\n4. **`alterShareGroupOffsets` - when `metadataImage == null`** - The `alterShareGroupOffsets` method checks both `!isActive.get()` and `metadataImage == null` in the same condition, and there's no test that specifically checks when coordinator is active but `metadataImage` is null.\n\n5. **`onResignation` when coordinator is active but partitions are being resigned mid-operation** - There's testing for onResignation with OptionalInt empty, but not for the race condition where operations are in-flight when resignation happens. The behavior when `onResignation` is called while operations are running hasn't been tested.\n\n6. **`deleteGroups` when called with an empty list** - There's no test for when `deleteGroups` is called with an empty list.\n\n7. **`deleteShareGroupOffsets` - null resultHolder** - In `deleteShareGroupOffsetsState`, when `resultHolder` is null, it returns UNKNOWN_SERVER_ERROR.
